The grounds are fantastic - there are peacocks, black swans, huge koi, a natural lake, two swimming pools (one outside particularly impressive), kids playground, indoor children‚Äôs room for little children, well equipped gym. 
The room was really spacious with large swivel tv, Marshall Blu tooth speaker, nespresso machine and Artelier Cologne shower gel/shampoo/body lotion/conditioner and soap. 
The breakfast room has lovely comfy sofas as well as tables. Breakfast was good and we spent a long time in the mornings just enjoying a long leisurely breakfast looking out at the garden. 
The attention to detail was superb, little extra goodies and just a general feeling that it was a cared‚Äîabout place. 
Service was great, friendly and helpful but equally un-intrusive.  
This was such a nice experience as I‚Äôve previously booked weekends away in China at big brand hotels and been really disappointed so I was apprehensive. Rose Garden Resort did not disappoint, we felt it was like being in a European boutique style hotel. It was so refreshing. 
We were here when it was wet and cold and we still enjoyed it - relaxing with books and at the indoor pool. We popped out into Hangzhou for dinner using DiDi which was easy enough.
Highly recommended, we will be back again!

msg:Environment: Among hotels with the same price in Hangzhou, this one is the most cost-effective and has the best environment. Very suitable for parent-child activities. There are also many foreign customers.
Unlike other hotels, except for the rooms, lobby, and gym, there are no other places for entertainment. The first floor of this hotel is a wellness center with indoor and outdoor swimming pools. In this season, the temperature of the indoor swimming pool is 30 degrees, which is very comfortable. There is also a gym, children's play room, and body care center on the second floor. There is a huge lawn outside with several green peacocks, black swans and koi carps. Along the path, there is a dense forest in the hotel. There is a lake deep in the forest, there are also black swans, and there is a small boat, which is like a fairyland.
Service: Front desk interns Xiao Cheng and Xiaojiao are very patient, meticulous and gentle in their service, and the customer experience is super good.
There is an English breakfast room on the first floor of the hotel, where you can eat until 10:30. The decoration style is very British and the breakfast is exquisite.
The Chinese restaurant is open from noon to 2 pm. The portions of the dishes are large and the taste is very good.
We stayed in a room with a skylight on the roof on the third floor. When we pushed out the window, we could overlook the hotel's swimming pool and green space, as well as the distant mountains.
The hotel is very clean and tidy. Welcome snacks are delivered every day, and there are free black tea and capsule coffee in the room and in the lobby. There are also resting areas in the stairwell. When we stayed during the festival, we were given free moon cakes and an exquisite coffee set gift bag.
recommend

msg:I did a lot of strategies. I originally wanted to live next to the West Lake, but the better star-rated hotels next to the West Lake start at 1500. Later, I saw the recommended strategy from Xiaohongshu and chose the Rose Garden Resort Hotel with a beautiful environment.
The hotel is next to the Qiantang River, about 10 kilometers away from the West Lake, and it takes about 20-30 minutes to take a taxi. The nearby attractions include Songcheng Eternal Love (next to it), Faxi Temple (6km), Meijiawu (4km)
Rose Garden Hotel focuses on roses. There are many red roses planted in the whole manor, and the clusters are very beautiful. As soon as you enter the hotel, you can smell the aroma of rose essential oil, which is very comfortable (forgot to ask them before leaving what brand did you use)
The interior of the room is very large, it should be 40 square meters. The room is equipped with a capsule coffee machine, BASE audio system, and Dyson hair dryer. The washing and care equipment is Oulong, and the hand sanitizer and hand cream are Bulgari white tea. It is worthy of a star hotel. The environment and Hygiene is not to be picked
There is a gymnasium, indoor heated swimming pool and billiards downstairs in the hotel. You can experience it for free when you stay. There are very few people in the swimming pool. You can swim and occupy the entire swimming pool by yourself.
There is also breakfast on the second day. The breakfast is very delicious and there are many varieties. The staff are very considerate in introducing and reminding us. Five-star recommendation!
Here, I would like to thank the hotel staff Xiaojiao and Feihao. The service attitude is very good, and the questions and needs raised will be solved immediately. The Rose Garden Resort Hotel is really worth recommending! I will stay again next time I come to Hangzhou!
